speake lord grumedan answered galaor king cildadan wee goe salute maiesty good faith quoth grumedan hee ioyfull returne please ride acquaint therewith doe replied galaor wee follow yee grumedan returning king hauing obserued long conference two knight demanded arriuall sir answered grumedan one lord galaor hath brought yee king cildadan company quoth king possible yes verily replied grumedan said king highest good happe could befall let v therfore goe kindely welcome made towards hee beheld galaor king cildadan dismounted horse doe reuerence whereupon embraced cheerefull countenance might easily noted whole company pleasing arriuall next demaund concerthe auncient damosell came thither sir answered galaor found since hermitage neere adioyning accompanied twelue k young gentleman reacheth beyond good faith sir replied queene must needes thanke great paine haue taken seeing ready make amends fault wherein knight haue offended reason requires likewise pardon error woman thinkes madame answered florestan feele paine trauaile obeying regard admired beautie doth well deserue conduct farre better knight affording honour bind ye shalbe able satisfie let v breake talke said queene tell shall wee set forward iourney please madame answered florestan first quoth grumedan hold meere conuey wounded knight towne farre hence may well attended vntill bee able mount horsebacke let bee
